# Paradiso - Canto 15

### 1 Benigna volontade in che si liqua

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: Benign will in which is always liquefied
- **gemini1-ja**: 慈悲深い意志が溶け込んだその中で

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: Benign will in which dissolves
- **gemma3-ja**: 慈悲深い意志において、それは解ける
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>Benigna</td><td>volontade</td><td>in</td><td>che</td><td>si</td><td>liqua</td></tr>
<tr><th>Lemma</th><td>benigno</td><td>volontà</td><td>in</td><td>che</td><td>si</td><td>liquefare</td></tr>

<tr><th>English</th><td>benign</td><td>will</td><td>in</td><td>that</td><td>yes</td><td>melts</td></tr>
<tr><th>Latin</th><td>benignus</td><td>voluntas</td><td>in</td><td>quod</td><td>sic</td><td>liquefacere</td></tr>
<tr><th>Interlingua</th><td>benigne</td><td>voluntate</td><td>in</td><td>que</td><td>sic</td><td>liquefacer</td></tr>
<tr><th>French</th><td>bénigne</td><td>volonté</td><td>dans</td><td>que</td><td>oui</td><td>fond</td></tr>
<tr><th>Spanish</th><td>benigno</td><td>voluntad</td><td>en</td><td>que</td><td>sí</td><td>derrite</td></tr>
<tr><th>Portuguese</th><td>benigno</td><td>vontade</td><td>em</td><td>que</td><td>sim</td><td>derrete</td></tr>
<tr><th>Romanian</th><td>blând</td><td>voință</td><td>în</td><td>că</td><td>da</td><td>topește</td></tr>
<tr><th>Esperanto</th><td>benigna</td><td>volo</td><td>en</td><td>ke</td><td>jes</td><td>likviĝas</td></tr>
<tr><th>Derived</th><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td></tr>
<tr><th>Etymology</th><td>bene + gignere</td><td>voluntas</td><td>in</td><td>quae</td><td>se</td><td>liquidus + facere</td></tr>
</table>

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: Benevolent will in which it melts  
- **gptoss-ja**: 優しい意志の中でそれが溶ける

### 2 sempre l’amor che drittamente spira,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: the love that rightly inspires,
- **gemini1-ja**: 常に正しく吹き込む愛は

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: always the love that rightly breathes,
- **gemma3-ja**: 常に正しく燃える愛、
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>sempre</td><td>l'</td><td>amor</td><td>che</td><td>drittamente</td><td>spira</td></tr>

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: always the love that rightly breathes,  
- **gptoss-ja**: 常に正しく息吹く愛、

### 3 come cupidità fa ne la iniqua,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: as cupidity does in the iniquitous,
- **gemini1-ja**: 不正な者の中にある欲望のように

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: as desire does in the iniquitous,
- **gemma3-ja**: 不正において欲望がするように。
<table>
<tr><th>Word</th><td>come</td><td>cupidità</td><td>fa</td><td>ne</td><td>la</td><td>iniqua</td></tr>
<tr><th>Lemma</th><td>come</td><td>cupidità</td><td>fare</td><td>in+le</td><td>il</td><td>iniquo</td></tr>
<tr><th>Part of Speech</th><td>conjunction</td><td>noun</td><td>verb</td><td>preposition+article</td><td>article</td><td>adjective</td></tr>
<tr><th>Gender</th><td></td><td>f.</td><td></td><td>f.</td><td>f.</td><td>f.</td></tr>
<tr><th>Number</th><td></td><td>sg.</td><td>sg.</td><td>pl.</td><td>sg.</td><td>sg.</td></tr>
<tr><th>Person</th><td></td><td></td><td>3</td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr>
<tr><th>Tense</th><td></td><td></td><td>present</td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr>

<tr><th>Latin</th><td>sicut</td><td>cupiditas</td><td>facere</td><td>non ille</td><td>ille</td><td>iniquus</td></tr>
<tr><th>Interlingua</th><td>como</td><td>cupiditate</td><td>facer</td><td>non le</td><td>le</td><td>inique</td></tr>
<tr><th>French</th><td>comme</td><td>cupidité</td><td>fait</td><td>pas le</td><td>le</td><td>inique</td></tr>
<tr><th>Spanish</th><td>como</td><td>codicia</td><td>hace</td><td>no el</td><td>el</td><td>inicuo</td></tr>

<tr><th>Romanian</th><td>ca</td><td>lăcomie</td><td>face</td><td>nu pe</td><td>pe</td><td>nedrept</td></tr>
<tr><th>Esperanto</th><td>kiel</td><td>avideco</td><td>faras</td><td>ne la</td><td>la</td><td>malbona</td></tr>
<tr><th>Derived</th><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Germanic</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td></tr>
<tr><th>Etymology</th><td>como</td><td>cupiditas</td><td>\*farjanan</td><td>ille</td><td>ille</td><td>iniquus</td></tr>
</table>

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: as cupidity does in the unjust,  
- **gptoss-ja**: 欲望が不正の中で行うように、

### 4 silenzio puose a quella dolce lira,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: imposed silence on that sweet lyre,
- **gemini1-ja**: その甘美な竪琴を沈黙させ

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: silence placed on that sweet lyre,
- **gemma3-ja**: それは甘いリラに沈黙を与え、

- **gptoss-en**: silence placed on that sweet lyre,  
- **gptoss-ja**: 沈黙がその甘いリラに置かれた、

### 6 che la destra del cielo allenta e tira.

- **gemini1-en**: that the right hand of heaven loosens and tightens.

- **gemma3-ja**: 終わりのない苦しみは良いことだ

### 18 nulla sen perde, ed esso dura poco:

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: nothing is lost, and it lasts a short time:
- **gemini1-ja**: 何も失われず、火は長く続かない。

### 39 ch’io non lo ’ntesi, sì parlò profondo;

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: which I did not understand, so profoundly did he speak;
- **gemini1-ja**: 私は理解できなかった。とても深く話したので。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: that I did not understand him, so deeply he spoke;
- **gemma3-ja**: 私はそれを理解できなかった、なぜなら彼は非常に深く話したから。

- **gemini1-en**: You believe that your thoughts come to me

### 57 da l’un, se si conosce, il cinque e ’l sei;

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: are derived from one, if one knows it;
- **gemini1-ja**: 五と六が分かるように。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: from the one, if it is known, the five and the six;
- **gemma3-ja**: 一つから五と六がわかるように、あなたに明らかだと信じている。

### 82 ond’ io, che son mortal, mi sento in questa

**gemini1-it**

- **gemini1-ja**: だから、私は死すべき者であるため、この

### 83 disagguaglianza, e però non ringrazio

**gemini1-it**

- **gemini1-ja**: 不平等を感じ、だから父なる祝宴に

### 84 se non col core a la paterna festa.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: only in my heart for the paternal feast.
- **gemini1-ja**: 心の中でしか感謝できない。

<tr><th>Word</th><td>se</td><td>non</td><td>col</td><td>core</td><td>a</td><td>la</td><td>paterna</td><td>festa</td></tr>

<tr><th>English</th><td>if</td><td>not</td><td>with the</td><td>heart</td><td>to</td><td>the</td><td>paternal</td><td>feast</td></tr>
<tr><th>Latin</th><td>si</td><td>non</td><td>cum + ille</td><td>cor</td><td>ad</td><td>ille</td><td>paternus</td><td>festa</td></tr>

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: if not with the heart to the paternal feast.
- **gemma3-ja**: 父なる祝祭に心で感謝しない限り。

### 90 cotal principio, rispondendo, femmi.

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: such was the beginning he made in answering me.
- **gemini1-ja**: そんな始まりを、答えて、彼女は私に告げた。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: such a beginning, responding, makes me.
- **gemma3-ja**: そのような始まりで、答えて、彼女は私にした。

### 96 tu li raccorci con l’opere tue.

### 148 e venni dal martiro a questa pace».
